Thank you Big John's Plumbing of Riverside for your speedy attention, dedication to detail and honesty.
It happened during a 16 hour power outage, our water heater died. Not sure if it was the power outage or the fourteen years it's been doing a great job of heating our water. Our son is a contractor and recommended we call Big John's Plumbing in Riverside. It was Saturday so we called and left a message. Someone at Big John's Plumbing called on Sunday morning and we confirmed that the repair could wait until Monday morning. Mr. Ramon showed up Monday and worked for three hours+ to replace the water heater. He ran into several non-compliance methods used when the original water heater was installed. He revised and installed the correct connections and insured we were up to code. We had hot water an hour after Mr. Ramon's departure.

We would recommend Big John's Plumbing, for any of your plumbing needs, I'm sure, but especially if you are in need of a new water heater. They've got you covered.<//review>

<Review>I haven't played or shopped here in a while on account of moving across the state but I'd recommend this shop to anyone I know purely based in knowing the owner.

Corey is a great guy who was running a great shop last I left it.

He has fair prices, listens to the community that plays at his shop and just genuinely cares about providing a good experience to his customers.

Last I was there the place was a little small and under renovations but I'm sure by now the place is looking spiffy.

I have lived in LA now for almost 8 months and have yet to find a shop that comes close to Corey's shop in terms of all around experience.

The only negative I have or had against the shop was just general size of the shop and it's general location, but you can't always get everything you want.

Oh also last I checked he was very active in getting different community events, games and different formats going.

< review>
this is the only place to go for all your MTG needs as well as many other similar games an collectables. Corey is a great guy an knows his stuff, he is always willing to answer any questions you may have. he shares a passion for the products an games he sells many nights you'll find him sitting at the tables playing right along with many of his more regular patrons laughing an joking along you could easily mistake him for just another player there trying out their new mtg deck build an having fun with good friends. Cory also buys cards as well an from my experience his shop is by far the best place to sell mtg cards, he always has the fairest offers an wont try to get one over on you ever. he is a kind an honest shop owner an really just wants to share his passion with as many as he can. If you do plan to sell cards here I would suggest selling to Corey directly as his other Mainstay employee has at times tends to be a little less fair an honest about his offers an rarely takes time to make sure the customer isn't being taken advantage of due to them simply being ignorant of card values an how card shops work. bottom line is when it comes to card shops ill take Cory's card shop over any big name shop like,  A1 Comics an others like them, ANY & EVERYTIME without a second thought. ive been a customer here since Cory's opened his shop an have loved it ever since. Not to mention that the location holds a special place in my heart as the card shop that was there many years prior to Cory's opening, was actually where my love hate relationship with Magic the Gathering all began back in February of 1998 id just turned 9 an with my birthday money i purchased my first ever booster pack of MTG. the set was stronghold an rightfully so it seem because MTG has had a strong hold over me ever since.<//review>

<pictures>None</pictures><Rating>4</Rating>< Review>
This was my first visit to Greek Chicken. I used the drive through and ordered a gyro sandwich, fried zucchini and a medium unsweetened ice tea. The gyro sandwich was one of the best I've had. The meat had great flavor, and the tomatoes and onions were fresh. Their tzatziki sauce is thick and flavorful! No runny sauce here!
The medium size drink could be a few ounces larger. The fried zucchini was Hot and a generous portion. Really like it being in a cup that fit in my car's cup holder. So, the reason for 4 stars: the fried zucchini. It is more breading than zucchini, but the flavor was really good! I'm a veggie fanatic so I do like to have lots of veggie under the breading.</Review>

<Name>Bob Arii</Name><Time>1563932694864</Time><Rating>5</Rating><review>We have  been coming to this recently updated, delicious place for many decades.  While the food may seem to cost a bit more, the quality and size of the portions are well worth it.

You order at the counter, fill your drink, get seated and wait for your number to be called..and if needed they will help yo carry your order to your table.

The salad are fresh and crisp.  While the chicken breast tends to be a bit dry, the other 'parts' are moist, delicious and have a tinge of lemony goodness that Greek chicken is known for...and the gyros (prounouced yeer-ohs) are simply spectacular!!!  I love to save some to put in a breakfast omelet with feta cheese.  Oh man!!!  Talk about heavenly leftovers!?!?!  I drool and dream for the next day to arrive.

The soft serve there is creamy and udderly (intended pun) decadent for the price!  Holy cow you've got to try it!!!

Should you like a bit better deal, you can order a half pound of Gyros meat and a half or full chicken, some pita bread and Tzatziki and a large Greek salad and feed 6 as long as they are not from a football team.

Fresh.  Flavorful.  Filling.  You can't go wrong if you stop to eat at Greek Chicken, Santee/El Cajon!!!</review><Pics>None<//Pics>< response>

< Review>
I love this place and have been coming for years.  The Gyros is as good as it gets and the chicken is really, really good.  The salads are also first rate.   Don't want bread?  Get the Gyros salad.  Even the small is a lot of food.  This is Gyros cut right from the spit...the only "real" Gyros!

Downside?  The Onion Rings are terrible.  I mean really bad.  Tasteless is the problem.  Obviously frozen and not fresh.  The Fries are ok.  Nothing to yell about, but ok.

Down and Dirty:  If you like GREEK...then stay with the Greek stuff on the menu.  Again, the Gyros is really first rate.  Expensive?  Yeh, I guess.  But, I've gotten Gyros in Plaza places that was cut, formed and had to be heated on the grill.

Oh, their yogurt sauce is spectacular if you are into that.

Best,</Review>
